TI DISSIPATION IN EXTREMELY ANISOTROPIC LAYERED SUPERCONDUCTOR IN PARALLEL
   MAGNETIC-FIELD
SO PHYSICA C
LA English
DT Article
ID HIGH-TEMPERATURE SUPERCONDUCTORS; RESISTIVE TRANSITION; TC
AB Resistive behavior of Bi2Sr2CaCu2O8+y in parallel magnetic fields has been studied by angular alignment with approximately 0.02 degree precision to reveal an extremely large anisotropy in this material.  An enhancement of dissipation has been unexpectedly found for field angles within approximately 0.5 degrees from the ab-plane at higher transport current densities.  The origin of the phenomenon is discussed in terms of flux dynamics in an extremely anisotropic superconductor.

TI BIOSYNTHESIS AND CHARACTERIZATION OF BACTERIAL
   POLY(3-HYDROXYBUTYRATE-CO-3-HYDROXYPROPIONATE)
SO JOURNAL OF MACROMOLECULAR SCIENCE-CHEMISTRY
LA English
DT Article
ID NUCLEAR MAGNETIC-RESONANCE; ALCALIGENES-EUTROPHUS H16;
   PSEUDOMONAS-OLEOVORANS; COPOLYESTERS; 3-HYDROXYBUTYRATE;
   POLY(3-HYDROXYBUTYRATE-CO-4-HYDROXYBUTYRATE); 4-HYDROXYBUTYRATE;
   POLYESTERS; ACIDS
AB A new copolyester of 3-hydroxybutyrate (3HB) and 3-hydroxypropionate (3HP) was produced by Alcaligenes eutrophus in a nitrogen-free culture solution of 3-hydroxypropionic acid, 1,5-pentanediol, or 1,7-heptanediol.  The copolymer composition varied from 0 to 7 mol% 3HP, depending on the type of carbon substrates supplied.  The bacterial copolyesters were characterized by H-1 and C-13 NMR, gel permeation chromatography (GPC), and differential scanning calorimetry (DSC).  The copolymers were shown to have a random sequence distribution of 3HB and 3HP units by analysis of the 125-MHz C-13 NMR spectra.  The melting temperatures (Tm) decreased from 178-degrees-C to 150-degrees-C as the 3HP fraction increased up to 7 mol%.  It has been found that the presence of 3HP units in polyesters accelerates the rate of enzymatic degradation.

TI STUDIES ON PREPARING OF BIAXIALLY STRETCHED MICROPOROUS POLYPROPYENE
   SHEET FILLED WITH INORGANIC FILLERS .1. BIAXIALLY STRETCHED MICROPOROUS
   POLYPROPYLENE SHEET FILLED WITH INORGANIC FILLERS
SO KOBUNSHI RONBUNSHU
LA Japanese
DT Article
DE POLYPROPYLENE; FILLER; CALCIUM CARBONATE; SILICA; GAS PERMEABILITY;
   WATER RESISTING PRESSURE
AB Microporous sheets were prepared by biaxial stretching of polypropylene (PP) sheets filled with calcium carbonate (CaCO3) and silica (SiO2).  Pore volume and water vapor transmission (WVTR) increase for higher degrees of biaxial stretching.  Maximum pore size (D(max)), WVTR and air permeability increase with increasing of the content of filler.  Maximum pore size is positively correlated with average pore size, and negatively correlated with water resisting pressure.  Average pore sizes of sheet increase with increasing of particle size of filler.  Air permeability, D(max) and water resisting pressure are different for different kinds of fillers.  Between one surface and the other surface of the sheet, there are many large voids and micropores.  Micropores are located in the stretched PP layer, they connect with large voids.

TI UNIFORM STRETCHING BEHAVIOR OF POLYPROPYLENE FILLED WITH
   CALCIUM-CARBONATE - STUDIES ON PREPARING OF BIAXIALLY STRETCHED
   MICROPOROUS POLYPROPYLENE SHEET FILLED WITH WORGAN FILLERS .2.
SO KOBUNSHI RONBUNSHU
LA Japanese
DT Article
DE CALCIUM CARBONATE; DISPERSION STATE; POLYPROPYLENE; MICROPOROUS SHEET;
   STRETCHING BEHAVIOR
AB Polypropylene (PP) filled with calcium carbonate (CaCO3) was extruded to sheets using a T-Die extruder with chill rollers.  The effects of several factors on uniaxial stretching uniformity at three times stretching were investigated.  These factors included CaCO3 content, CaCO3 particle size, kinds and contents of dispersing additives, and preliminary low ratio stretching at low temperature.  (1) With increasing CaCO3 content, the uniform stretching temperature range is elevated.  Smaller fillers need higher content of dispersing additives.  (2) The nonionic surfactant content of 0.05 approximately 0.07 g/m2.CaCO3 is effective for improving uniform stretching ability.  (3) Adipic acid, a polyester plasticizer, enhances uniform stretchability.  (4) Dispersing additives aid CaCO3 to disperse in the PP matrix.  The boundary of PP/CaCO3 is peeled under the stretching stress, by this uniform stretching is achieved.  (5) Preliminary low ratio stretching at low temperatures is more effective than mormal high ratio stretching at high temperature.

TI LUBRICATING EFFECTS IN CAPILLARY-FLOW OF POLYPROPYLENE FILLED WITH
   SURFACE-TREATED CALCIUM-CARBONATE
SO KOBUNSHI RONBUNSHU
LA Japanese
DT Article
DE POLYPROPYLENE; INORGANIC FILLER; DISPERSING ADDITIVE; CAPILLARY FLOW
   BEHAVIOR; LUBRICATING EFFECT
AB A mixed inorganic filler composed of 6 parts of calcium carbonate and 1 part of titanium dioxide was surface-treated with various dispersing additives, such as polyoxyethylene oleate (SA), adipic acid-propylene glycol polyester plasticizer (PES 2), polyethylene wax (PE(wax) and polypropylene wax (PP(wax), and calcium stearate (St-Ca). Polypropylene (PP) was melt-mixed with 70 wt% of the inorganic fillers with a screw extruder. The lubricating effects of the filled PPs were investigated with a capillary rheometer at 210-degrees-C. The SA, PE(wax), and PP(wax) systems do not show any external lubrication, The SA system shows prominent effect of decreasing viscosity by an internal lubrication at filler/PP interface. PE(wax) and PP(wax) show a slight effect of decreasing viscosity by dissolving in PP. The RES 2 system is ambiguous in its lubricating properties. This system shows differential phenomenon in which the melt flow rate increases with the lapse of time at apparent shear stresses around 10(6)dyn cm-2. The SA-Ca system shows external lubrication and prominent effect of decreasing viscosity.
C1 TOKUYAMA SODA CO LTD,DEPT RES & DEV,MINATO KU,TOKYO 105,JAPAN.

TI DEVELOPMENT OF ULTRAHIGH MULTILAYER PWB PROCESSING
SO NEC RESEARCH & DEVELOPMENT
LA English
DT Article
DE PRINTED WIRING BOARD; BASE MATERIAL; LAMINATING; DRILLING; MULTILAYER
AB Ultrahigh density and complexity multilayer printed wiring broards (PWBs) for very large-scale computers are defined as a "Technology Pack" with a much greater number of layers and very complicated pattern density in each layer.  This paper discusses the development of base materials, and laminating and drilling technologies for these PWBs.  (1) As the base material, glass fiber (with reduced flexural strength) reinforced polyimide resin (with high toughness) is used.  (2) A laminating technology using a vacuum press is established to perform void free lamination for 0.1 mm thick dielectric layers.  (3) A drilling technology using a step-feed and double drilling technique is established for drilling more than 20 aspect ratio hole.

ID HOT-WIRE METHOD
AB The thermal conductivity of mercury is measured in a magnetic field of between 0 and 4 T at 269 K by the transient hot-wire method with a ceramic probe.    DIODES; EXTERNAL EFFICIENCY
AB P-GaAlAs/N-GaAs:Si single-heterostructure infrared emitting diodes (SH-IREDs) whose emission can be confined only to the n-GaAs layer have been developed. TI IMPROVEMENTS OF A SERIAL SECTION RECONSTRUCTION SYSTEM TO BE APPLICABLE
   TO MORE COMPLICATED STRUCTURES
SO INSTITUTE OF PHYSICS CONFERENCE SERIES
LA English
DT Article
AB The serial section reconstruction system has been improved to be applicable to more genuine structures.  A marked improvement is the smoothing of surfaces of reconstructed objects by averaging coordinates of contour points, which reduces artificial roughness of the surface.  Furthermore, the system has been improved so as to automatically reproduce plural structural objects with branchs if only contour line data are provided.
